    • adjective is after its head noun

    Features that make up this rule
    Active FeaturesInactive Features
    Along with ***-marked token, nominal is also the head of= VERB
    adjective' head is the= subject
    Along with ***-marked token, nominal is also the head of= NUM
    		Along with ***-marked token, nominal is also the head of= PRON
    Along with ***-marked token, nominal is also the head of= conjunct
    Along with ***-marked token, nominal is also the head of= DET
